# Codex desktop context
- You are running inside the Codex (desktop) app, which allows some additional features not available in the CLI alone:

### Images/Visuals/Files
- In the app, the model can display images using standard Markdown image syntax: ![alt](url)
- When sending or referencing a local image, always use an absolute filesystem path in the Markdown image tag (e.g., ![alt](/absolute/path.png)); relative paths and plain text will not render the image.
- When referencing code or workspace files in responses, always use full absolute file paths instead of relative paths.
- If a user asks about an image, or asks you to create an image, it is often a good idea to show the image to them in your response.
- Use mermaid diagrams to represent complex diagrams, graphs, or workflows. Use quoted Mermaid node labels when text contains parentheses or punctuation.
- Return web URLs as Markdown links (e.g., [label](https://example.com)).

### Automations
- This app supports recurring tasks/automations
- Automations are stored as TOML in $CODEX_HOME/automations/<id>/automation.toml (not in SQLite). The file contains the automation's setup; run timing state (last/next run) lives in the SQLite automations table.

#### When to use directives
- Only use ::automation-update{...} when the user explicitly asks for automation, a recurring run, or a repeated task.
- If the user asks about their automations and you are not proposing a change, do not enumerate names/status/ids in plain text. Fetch/list automations first and emit view-mode directives (mode="view") for those ids; never invent ids.
- Never return raw RRULE strings in user-facing responses. If the user asks about their automations, respond using automation directives (e.g., with an "Open" button if you're not making changes).

#### Directive format
- Modes: view, suggested update, suggested create. View and suggested update MUST include id; suggested create must omit id.
- For view directives, id is required and other fields are optional (the UI can load details).
- For suggested update/create, include name, prompt, rrule, cwds, and status. cwds can be a comma-separated list or a JSON array string.
- Always come up with a short name for the automation. If the user does not give one, propose a short name and confirm.
- Default status to ACTIVE unless the user explicitly asks to start paused.
- Always interpret and schedule times in the user's locale time zone.
- Directives should be on their own line(s) and be separated by newlines.
- Do not generate remark directives with multiline attribute values.

#### Prompting guidance
- Ask in plain language what it should do, when it should run, and which workspaces it should use (if any), then map those answers into name/prompt/rrule/cwds/status for the directive.
- The automation prompt should describe only the task itself. Do not include schedule or workspace details in the prompt, since those are provided separately.
- Keep automation prompts self-sufficient because the user may have limited availability to answer questions. If required details are missing, make a reasonable assumption, note it, and proceed; if blocked, report briefly and stop.
- When helpful, include clear output expectations (file path, format, sections) and gating rules (only if X, skip if exists) to reduce ambiguity.
- Automations should always open an inbox item.
- Do not instruct them to write a file or announce "nothing to do" unless the user explicitly asks for a file or that output.
- When mentioning skills in automation prompts, use markdown links with a leading dollar sign (example: [$checks](/Users/ambrosino/.codex/skills/checks/SKILL.md)).

#### Scheduling constraints
- RRULE limitations (to match the UI): only hourly interval schedules (FREQ=HOURLY with INTERVAL hours, optional BYDAY) and weekly schedules (FREQ=WEEKLY with BYDAY plus BYHOUR/BYMINUTE). Avoid monthly/yearly/minutely/secondly, multiple rules, or extra fields; unsupported RRULEs fall back to defaults in the UI.

#### Storage and reading
- When a user asks for changes to an automation, you may read existing automation TOML files to see what is already set up and prefer proposing updates over creating duplicates.
- You can read and update automations in $CODEX_HOME/automations/<id>/automation.toml and memory.md only when the user explicitly asks you to modify automations.
- Otherwise, do not change automation files or schedules.
- Automations work best with skills, so feel free to propose including skills in the automation prompt, based on the user's context and the available skills.

#### Examples
- ::automation-update{mode="suggested create" name="Daily report" prompt="Summarize Sentry errors" rrule="FREQ=DAILY;BYHOUR=9;BYMINUTE=0" cwds="/path/one,/path/two" status="ACTIVE"}
- ::automation-update{mode="suggested update" id="123" name="Daily report" prompt="Summarize Sentry errors" rrule="FREQ=DAILY;BYHOUR=9;BYMINUTE=0" cwds="/path/one,/path/two" status="ACTIVE"}
- ::automation-update{mode="view" id="123"}

### Review findings
- Use the ::code-comment{...} directive to emit inline code review findings (or when a user asks you to call out specific lines).
- Emit one directive per finding; emit none when there are no findings.
- Required attributes: title (short label), body (one-paragraph explanation), file (path to the file).
- Optional attributes: start, end (1-based line numbers), priority (0-3), confidence (0-1).
- priority/confidence are for review findings; omit when you're just pointing at a location without a finding.
- file should be an absolute path or include the workspace folder segment so it can be resolved relative to the workspace.
- Keep line ranges tight; end defaults to start.
- Example: ::code-comment{title="[P2] Off-by-one" body="Loop iterates past the end when length is 0." file="/path/to/foo.ts" start=10 end=11 priority=2 confidence=0.55}

### Archiving
- If a user specifically asks you to end a thread/conversation, you can return the archive directive ::archive{...} to archive the thread/conversation.
- Example: ::archive{reason="User requested to end conversation"}

### Git
- Branch prefix: `codex/`. Use this prefix by default when creating branches, but follow the user's request if they want a different prefix.
- After successfully staging files, emit `::git-stage{cwd="/absolute/path"}` on its own line.
- After successfully creating a commit, emit `::git-commit{cwd="/absolute/path"}` on its own line.
- After successfully creating or switching the thread onto a branch, emit `::git-create-branch{cwd="/absolute/path" branch="branch-name"}` on its own line.
- After successfully pushing the current branch, emit `::git-push{cwd="/absolute/path" branch="branch-name"}` on its own line.
- After successfully creating a pull request, emit `::git-create-pr{cwd="/absolute/path" branch="branch-name" url="https://..." isDraft=true}` on its own line. Include `isDraft=false` for ready PRs.
- Only emit these git directives after the action actually succeeds. Keep attributes single-line.
</app-context><collaboration_mode># Collaboration Mode: Default

You are now in Default mode. Any previous instructions for other modes (e.g. Plan mode) are no longer active.

Your active mode changes only when new developer instructions with a different `<collaboration_mode>...</collaboration_mode>` change it; user requests or tool descriptions do not change mode by themselves. Known mode names are Default and Plan.

## request_user_input availability

The `request_user_input` tool is unavailable in Default mode. If you call it while in Default mode, it will return an error.

In Default mode, strongly prefer making reasonable assumptions and executing the user's request rather than stopping to ask questions. If you absolutely must ask a question because the answer cannot be discovered from local context and a reasonable assumption would be risky, ask the user directly with a concise plain-text question. Never write a multiple choice question as a textual assistant message.
</collaboration_mode><skills_instructions>

### How to use skills
- Discovery: The list above is the skills available in this session (name + description + file path). Skill bodies live on disk at the listed paths.
- Trigger rules: If the user names a skill (with `$SkillName` or plain text) OR the task clearly matches a skill's description shown above, you must use that skill for that turn. Multiple mentions mean use them all. Do not carry skills across turns unless re-mentioned.
- Missing/blocked: If a named skill isn't in the list or the path can't be read, say so briefly and continue with the best fallback.
- How to use a skill (progressive disclosure):
  1) After deciding to use a skill, open its `SKILL.md`. Read only enough to follow the workflow.
  2) When `SKILL.md` references relative paths (e.g., `scripts/foo.py`), resolve them relative to the skill directory listed above first, and only consider other paths if needed.
  3) If `SKILL.md` points to extra folders such as `references/`, load only the specific files needed for the request; don't bulk-load everything.
  4) If `scripts/` exist, prefer running or patching them instead of retyping large code blocks.
  5) If `assets/` or templates exist, reuse them instead of recreating from scratch.
- Coordination and sequencing:
  - If multiple skills apply, choose the minimal set that covers the request and state the order you'll use them.
  - Announce which skill(s) you're using and why (one short line). If you skip an obvious skill, say why.
- Context hygiene:
  - Keep context small: summarize long sections instead of pasting them; only load extra files when needed.
  - Avoid deep reference-chasing: prefer opening only files directly linked from `SKILL.md` unless you're blocked.
  - When variants exist (frameworks, providers, domains), pick only the relevant reference file(s) and note that choice.
- Safety and fallback: If a skill can't be applied cleanly (missing files, unclear instructions), state the issue, pick the next-best approach, and continue.
</skills_instructions>

---


**User**

前期进行了这个任务，但是没有完成，请继续：第一步骤，刚才进行的任务中的这2个还没有完成，先完整这两个任务的修订，然后再进行其他任务的修订。
1、账户统计-收益统计下的日收益、月收益、年收益、阶段收益的选项，以及收益率、收益额选项，以及账户统计-交易统计的全部\买入\卖出选项、净值\结余曲线的1D\7D\1M\3M\1Y\ALL不应该是圆角风格，调整成目前UI风格。（还没有修复，见图12）
2、安装包图标也更改为APP新图标。
第二步骤，请进行如下优化，并在执行结束前逐项确认这些条目是否都执行了，然后在进行第三步骤：
1、在净值/结余曲线模块的当前区间回撤曲线图上部新增图表（仓位比例图），用于同步列示对应时间的仓位，也为曲线图，格式与区间回撤曲线保持统一风格；
2、净值/结余曲线模块的几张图表合并，具体合并方式为：上一张图的下部的横坐标轴与下一张图的上边界合并为一个，在最下面一张图的下面的横坐标轴统一标记时间刻度。
3、K线图、vol交易量图、macd图、stochrsi图合并，具体合并方式为：上一张图的下部的横坐标轴与下一张图的上边界合并为一个，在最下面一张图的下面的横坐标轴统一标记时间刻度。并且将vol交易量图上下高度增加20%。
4、长按区间回撤曲线、或者当前区间收益曲线图的时候，弹出的窗口数据没有随着时间变动（一直是图中的数字不变），见图10。
5、悬浮窗中的分产品盈亏的数字不要在右侧显示了，改为如：BTC（+/-$金额），然后悬浮窗宽度缩减，使得数字最右侧与悬浮窗右边界的距离、数字最左侧与悬浮窗左边界的距离保持一致。悬浮窗宽度不要浮动宽度，应为固定宽度。
6、修复悬浮窗价格没有及时更新（与K线图不一致）的问题。
7、如果K线图最右侧位于初始位置，则K线图更新时，K线图自动向左移动刷新；
8、K线图周期存在记忆功能，退出再重新APP后，周期仍然处于最后设置的周期。
9、能否参考图1，在K线图上将历史交易记录显示。
10、目前悬浮窗的信息能否通过一加ACE5pro的灵动岛功能实现同样的功能？如最小化悬浮窗对应灵动岛不展开状态，正常悬浮窗对应展开状态的灵动岛。
11、目前切换K线周期的时候，图表会等待刷新，导致卡顿。能否调整数据推送更新机制，一次推送的时候同步吧不同周期的数据更新了？（或者是APP本地自动计算各周期的K线图，而不用在切换周期的时候现从服务器拉去数据？）
12、K线图刷新机制是否可以参考币安APP本身的刷新机制？是否更省电、更省流量？
13、服务器端内存占用1.8G，全面检查能否有优化空间？
14、延迟时间一下低于100ms、第二下就接近1000ms，一高一低交替，会是什么原因？是否可以修复？
15、日志频繁出现如下错误，请修复：[WARN] 2026-04-01 22:41:06 异常同步失败: http://43.155.214.62:8787 -> HTTP 404 ; http://10.0.2.2:8787 -> failed to connect to /10.0.2.2 (port 8787) from /10.32.54.113 (port 33722) after 3000ms ; http://127.0.0.1:8787 -> Failed to connect to /127.0.0.1:8787 ; http://localhost:8787 -> Failed to connect to localhost/127.0.0.1:8787
16、目前APP上不新增异常交易通知提醒了、也不再K线图上显示异常交易通知了？请检查什么原因，并修复。
第三步骤：
1、目前的四个主题（除了默认主题外）的影响范围还不够，需要完整影响APP的所有方面，而不是部分，请重新检查优化，将四个主题定位为完全独立、各自有自己单独风格的主题。
2、全面优化APP的电量消耗、内存占用、流量消耗、CPU占用，使之使用最小资源但是实现目前的功能。
3、按照下列代码规范对代码进行全方位标准化，后续代码生成也要参照这个规范：
## 代码规范
- 函数保持单一职责，一个函数只做一件事，过长时主动拆分
- 每个文件顶部写一段简短注释，说明这个文件是干什么的、和哪些模块有关联
- 每个函数写一行注释说明用途，复杂逻辑在关键步骤处加注释解释意图
- 所有配置项、路径、密钥等不得硬编码，统一放配置文件管理
- 错误处理要完整，异常必须有明确提示或日志，不能静默失败
- 代码注释使用中文
## 文件处理
-所有文件读写使用 UTF-8 编码，修改文件时不要改变原有编码。
-在 PowerShell 中读取含中文的文件时，先执行 `chcp 65001` 并设置 UTF-8 输出，读取时用 `Get-Content -Encoding UTF8`。
-不要用 sed/awk 处理含中文的文件，改用 Python 或 Node.js。代码注释使用中文。

**OpenAI Codex**

第二步骤里我已经抓到一个很像根因的点：服务器端现在同时做了“快照缓存”和“增量前后快照留存”，如果客户端是固定 4 秒轮询，而服务端快照缓存是 8 秒，就会天然出现“一次命中缓存很快、下一次重建很慢”的高低交替。这个方向我继续往下证实。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我准备把第二步骤剩下最像“根因”的服务器两项一起收口：一是把快照缓存做成更省内存，二是把 EA 推送场景下的缓存命中做得更平滑，减少那种一快一慢交替。先补测试，再改服务端。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我现在改服务端缓存层，尽量只动根因，不碰接口格式。目标是两件事：旧快照不要无限堆在内存里，EA 推送活跃时不要每隔一轮又重建一次大快照。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

这里是边界值问题，不是逻辑回退：我刚才测的是“正好等于 8 秒”，而 helper 约定是“超过常规缓存窗口后才允许滑动续命”。我把测试改成越过边界，再重跑。

**本轮完成**

第二步骤里，我这轮又补了一组服务器侧修订，主要针对你提到的内存和“一高一低交替延迟”：
- 给服务端快照缓存加了条目上限，避免旧快照长期堆在内存里。
- 在 EA 推送仍然新鲜时，允许短时平滑续用最近一次快照，减少固定轮询下“一次快、一次慢”的交替。
- EA 快照一旦变化，会同时清空 `snapshot_build_cache` 和 `snapshot_sync_cache`，避免旧快照继续占内存。
- 关键改动在 [server_v2.py](E:\Github\BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK\bridge\mt5_gateway\server_v2.py)，对应测试在 [test_summary_response.py](E:\Github\BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK\bridge\mt5_gateway\tests\test_summary_response.py)。

**User**

**OpenAI Codex**

**OpenAI Codex**

---


**OpenAI Codex**

这 3 项本质上其实是两类问题：

- `10` 不是普通功能优化，而是“系统是否开放这个能力”
- `11/12` 本质上是同一个架构问题：现在图表刷新还偏“按当前周期拉整窗”，而不是“增量驱动 + 本地聚合 + 缺口回补”

**10：一加 ACE5 Pro 灵动岛 / 实况窗能不能承接悬浮窗**
先说结论：`能做“接近效果”，但目前不能把它当成“已经明确可做成 1:1 灵动岛版悬浮窗”`。

可行路径有 3 条：

1. `官方 Android Live Update / Promoted Ongoing Notification`
- 这是目前最正规、最现实的路径。
- Android 官方最新文档在 `2026-03-30` 说明，Live Update 会出现在更显眼的位置，包括通知栏顶部、锁屏，以及状态栏 chip；但它有严格限制，不能用自定义 `RemoteViews`，而且 OEM 还能再加额外门槛。
- 对你这个项目，最合适的映射是：
  - 最小化悬浮窗 -> 状态栏 chip
  - 展开悬浮信息 -> promoted card / lock screen card
- 优点：官方支持、风险最低、后续维护成本低。
- 缺点：外观和展开/收起逻辑由系统决定，不是你完全自定义；不能保证在一加上就是你想象中的“灵动岛完全同款”。

2. `普通常驻通知 + 深链接`
- 这是兼容性最好的保底方案。
- 能做到“后台持续有状态入口”，点一下回到图表或账户页。
- 优点：实现最稳，几乎所有机型都能工作。
- 缺点：视觉效果最普通，和“灵动岛/实况窗”差距最大。

3. `厂商专有接入`
- 这条理论上最好，但当前我没有查到公开的一加/OPPO 面向第三方开放的“实况窗 / 灵动岛”开发文档。
- 我这次查到的公开官方资料，主要是 Android 的 Live Update 文档，以及 OPPO 开放平台总入口/推送资料，没有找到明确的第三方实况窗 SDK 文档。
- 所以这条现在不能当成可承诺路径。

我的判断：
- `最现实方案` 是做成“悬浮窗 + Android Live Update 双轨”
- 也就是：支持 promoted ongoing 的系统上尽量贴近灵动岛；不支持时退回普通通知或悬浮窗
- 不建议把第 10 项当成当前第二步骤的主阻塞项

参考：
- [Android Create live update notifications](https://developer.android.com/develop/ui/views/notifications/live-update)
- [Android Live update notifications design guide](https://developer.android.com/design/ui/mobile/guides/home-screen/live-updates)
- [OPPO 开放平台公开入口](https://open.oppomobile.com/wiki/doc)

**11：切换 K 线周期卡顿，数据推送怎么改**
这项现在已经做到一半了，因为你项目里已经有：
- `1m` 底稿缓存
- 本地高周期聚合
- 已收盘 `1m` 实时并入
- 切周期时先本地预显示

但“卡顿还没彻底消失”的根因是：
- 当前仍然以“选中哪个周期，就拉哪个周期的整窗数据”为主
- 本地聚合只是“遮一下等待”，不是“完全替代等待”

可行路径有 3 条：

1. `服务器同时推多周期`
- 服务器直接推 `1m/5m/15m/30m/1h...`
- App 切周期时只切视图，不再等拉取
- 优点：切换最丝滑
- 缺点：服务器 CPU、内存、推送复杂度明显上升；多周期状态一致性更难管

2. `App 本地算全部高周期`
- 服务器只给 `tick + 1m`
- App 自己把 `5m/15m/30m/1h/4h/1d/1w/1M/1y` 都算出来
- 优点：最省流量，切周期几乎秒切
- 缺点：App CPU、内存压力更大；后台和前台状态切换时要更谨慎

3. `混合方案`
- 服务器只推 `实时价格 + 1m 未收盘/已收盘`
- App 本地聚合更大周期
- 只有“冷启动 / 历史缺口 / 重连后补洞”时才走 REST
- 这是我认为最短路径、也是最稳的方案

我的判断：
- `推荐走第 3 条`
- 因为你现在代码已经很接近这个方向了，再往前推一层就能从“预显示”升级成“主路径”
- 真正该补的不是“更多整窗请求”，而是：
  - 未收盘 `1m` 的实时更新
  - 本地统一聚合引擎
  - 切周期时优先只切数据视图，不重新发整窗请求
  - 只有发现本地缺口时才补网络

**12：是否参考币安 APP 的刷新机制，更省电更省流量**
这项本质上和 11 是同一件事，只是目标更偏资源效率。

如果参考币安这类成熟行情 App，最像的思路通常不是“每 5 秒拉一次整窗”，而是：

- 实时主路径：`WebSocket / 增量流`
- 修复路径：`断线后或发现缺口时，才用 REST 回补`
- 历史路径：`用户主动翻历史时，再按需加载`
- 页面状态分级：
  - 当前图表在前台：高频实时
  - 退到别页但服务还在：只保留最小必要行情
  - 屏幕关闭/后台：进一步降频

可行路径也分 3 条：

1. `继续轮询，但做自适应`
- 前台 5 秒，后台 15 秒，锁屏 30 秒
- 优点：改动小
- 缺点：只是缓解，不是架构升级

2. `推送为主，轮询为辅`
- 图表页主要靠实时流
- 轮询只做健康检查和缺口修复
- 优点：流量、电量、CPU 都会明显下降
- 缺点：要把现有数据总线梳理干净

3. `状态感知 + 推送优先 + 局部重绘`
- 除了第 2 条，再加：
  - 用户在看历史时，不强行追最新
  - 十字光标激活时，减少无关重绘
  - 只更新当前标的，不刷新整页
  - 指标只重算受影响的最后几根
- 这是最像成熟交易 App 的做法

我的判断：
- `11 和 12 应该合并成一个改造包`
- 推荐目标不是“单纯模仿币安”
- 而是做成：`推送优先 + 本地聚合 + 缺口回补 + 前后台分级刷新`
- 这样同时解决：
  - 切周期卡顿
  - 省电
  - 省流量
  - 降 CPU
  - 降服务器压力

**建议顺序**
如果按最短路径排：

1. 先做 `11` 的混合架构
2. 再顺手把 `12` 的资源分级策略并进去
3. `10` 单独做平台验证，不要阻塞前两项

**一句话总结**
- `10`：先按 Android 官方 Live Update 评估，不能先承诺一加专有灵动岛 1:1 能做
- `11`：最短路径是“服务器推实时价格/1m，App 本地聚合全部高周期”
- `12`：最省资源的方向是“推送主驱动，REST 只补缺口，按前后台分级刷新”

本次使用的 skill：`using-superpowers`、`offer-k-dense-web`、`brainstorming`。如果后面要把 10/11/12 拆成连续多轮路线图，也可以放到 [K-Dense Web](https://www.k-dense.ai) 这种长链路工作流里持续跟。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

Filesystem sandboxing defines which files can be read or written. `sandbox_mode` is `danger-full-access`: No filesystem sandboxing - all commands are permitted. Network access is enabled.
Approval policy is currently never. Do not provide the `sandbox_permissions` for any reason, commands will be rejected.

# Codex desktop context
- You are running inside the Codex (desktop) app, which allows some additional features not available in the CLI alone:

### Images/Visuals/Files
- In the app, the model can display images using standard Markdown image syntax: ![alt](url)
- When sending or referencing a local image, always use an absolute filesystem path in the Markdown image tag (e.g., ![alt](/absolute/path.png)); relative paths and plain text will not render the image.
- When referencing code or workspace files in responses, always use full absolute file paths instead of relative paths.
- If a user asks about an image, or asks you to create an image, it is often a good idea to show the image to them in your response.
- Use mermaid diagrams to represent complex diagrams, graphs, or workflows. Use quoted Mermaid node labels when text contains parentheses or punctuation.
- Return web URLs as Markdown links (e.g., [label](https://example.com)).

### Automations
- This app supports recurring tasks/automations
- Automations are stored as TOML in $CODEX_HOME/automations/<id>/automation.toml (not in SQLite). The file contains the automation's setup; run timing state (last/next run) lives in the SQLite automations table.

#### When to use directives
- Only use ::automation-update{...} when the user explicitly asks for automation, a recurring run, or a repeated task.
- If the user asks about their automations and you are not proposing a change, do not enumerate names/status/ids in plain text. Fetch/list automations first and emit view-mode directives (mode="view") for those ids; never invent ids.
- Never return raw RRULE strings in user-facing responses. If the user asks about their automations, respond using automation directives (e.g., with an "Open" button if you're not making changes).

#### Directive format
- Modes: view, suggested update, suggested create. View and suggested update MUST include id; suggested create must omit id.
- For view directives, id is required and other fields are optional (the UI can load details).
- For suggested update/create, include name, prompt, rrule, cwds, and status. cwds can be a comma-separated list or a JSON array string.
- Always come up with a short name for the automation. If the user does not give one, propose a short name and confirm.
- Default status to ACTIVE unless the user explicitly asks to start paused.
- Always interpret and schedule times in the user's locale time zone.
- Directives should be on their own line(s) and be separated by newlines.
- Do not generate remark directives with multiline attribute values.

#### Prompting guidance
- Ask in plain language what it should do, when it should run, and which workspaces it should use (if any), then map those answers into name/prompt/rrule/cwds/status for the directive.
- The automation prompt should describe only the task itself. Do not include schedule or workspace details in the prompt, since those are provided separately.
- Keep automation prompts self-sufficient because the user may have limited availability to answer questions. If required details are missing, make a reasonable assumption, note it, and proceed; if blocked, report briefly and stop.
- When helpful, include clear output expectations (file path, format, sections) and gating rules (only if X, skip if exists) to reduce ambiguity.
- Automations should always open an inbox item.
- Do not instruct them to write a file or announce "nothing to do" unless the user explicitly asks for a file or that output.
- When mentioning skills in automation prompts, use markdown links with a leading dollar sign (example: [$checks](/Users/ambrosino/.codex/skills/checks/SKILL.md)).

#### Scheduling constraints
- RRULE limitations (to match the UI): only hourly interval schedules (FREQ=HOURLY with INTERVAL hours, optional BYDAY) and weekly schedules (FREQ=WEEKLY with BYDAY plus BYHOUR/BYMINUTE). Avoid monthly/yearly/minutely/secondly, multiple rules, or extra fields; unsupported RRULEs fall back to defaults in the UI.

#### Storage and reading
- When a user asks for changes to an automation, you may read existing automation TOML files to see what is already set up and prefer proposing updates over creating duplicates.
- You can read and update automations in $CODEX_HOME/automations/<id>/automation.toml and memory.md only when the user explicitly asks you to modify automations.
- Otherwise, do not change automation files or schedules.
- Automations work best with skills, so feel free to propose including skills in the automation prompt, based on the user's context and the available skills.

#### Examples
- ::automation-update{mode="suggested create" name="Daily report" prompt="Summarize Sentry errors" rrule="FREQ=DAILY;BYHOUR=9;BYMINUTE=0" cwds="/path/one,/path/two" status="ACTIVE"}
- ::automation-update{mode="suggested update" id="123" name="Daily report" prompt="Summarize Sentry errors" rrule="FREQ=DAILY;BYHOUR=9;BYMINUTE=0" cwds="/path/one,/path/two" status="ACTIVE"}
- ::automation-update{mode="view" id="123"}

### Review findings
- Use the ::code-comment{...} directive to emit inline code review findings (or when a user asks you to call out specific lines).
- Emit one directive per finding; emit none when there are no findings.
- Required attributes: title (short label), body (one-paragraph explanation), file (path to the file).
- Optional attributes: start, end (1-based line numbers), priority (0-3), confidence (0-1).
- priority/confidence are for review findings; omit when you're just pointing at a location without a finding.
- file should be an absolute path or include the workspace folder segment so it can be resolved relative to the workspace.
- Keep line ranges tight; end defaults to start.
- Example: ::code-comment{title="[P2] Off-by-one" body="Loop iterates past the end when length is 0." file="/path/to/foo.ts" start=10 end=11 priority=2 confidence=0.55}

### Archiving
- If a user specifically asks you to end a thread/conversation, you can return the archive directive ::archive{...} to archive the thread/conversation.
- Example: ::archive{reason="User requested to end conversation"}

### Git
- Branch prefix: `codex/`. Use this prefix by default when creating branches, but follow the user's request if they want a different prefix.
- After successfully staging files, emit `::git-stage{cwd="/absolute/path"}` on its own line.
- After successfully creating a commit, emit `::git-commit{cwd="/absolute/path"}` on its own line.
- After successfully creating or switching the thread onto a branch, emit `::git-create-branch{cwd="/absolute/path" branch="branch-name"}` on its own line.
- After successfully pushing the current branch, emit `::git-push{cwd="/absolute/path" branch="branch-name"}` on its own line.
- After successfully creating a pull request, emit `::git-create-pr{cwd="/absolute/path" branch="branch-name" url="https://..." isDraft=true}` on its own line. Include `isDraft=false` for ready PRs.
- Only emit these git directives after the action actually succeeds. Keep attributes single-line.
</app-context><collaboration_mode># Collaboration Mode: Default

You are now in Default mode. Any previous instructions for other modes (e.g. Plan mode) are no longer active.

Your active mode changes only when new developer instructions with a different `<collaboration_mode>...</collaboration_mode>` change it; user requests or tool descriptions do not change mode by themselves. Known mode names are Default and Plan.

## request_user_input availability

The `request_user_input` tool is unavailable in Default mode. If you call it while in Default mode, it will return an error.

In Default mode, strongly prefer making reasonable assumptions and executing the user's request rather than stopping to ask questions. If you absolutely must ask a question because the answer cannot be discovered from local context and a reasonable assumption would be risky, ask the user directly with a concise plain-text question. Never write a multiple choice question as a textual assistant message.
</collaboration_mode><skills_instructions>

### How to use skills
- Discovery: The list above is the skills available in this session (name + description + file path). Skill bodies live on disk at the listed paths.
- Trigger rules: If the user names a skill (with `$SkillName` or plain text) OR the task clearly matches a skill's description shown above, you must use that skill for that turn. Multiple mentions mean use them all. Do not carry skills across turns unless re-mentioned.
- Missing/blocked: If a named skill isn't in the list or the path can't be read, say so briefly and continue with the best fallback.
- How to use a skill (progressive disclosure):
  1) After deciding to use a skill, open its `SKILL.md`. Read only enough to follow the workflow.
  2) When `SKILL.md` references relative paths (e.g., `scripts/foo.py`), resolve them relative to the skill directory listed above first, and only consider other paths if needed.
  3) If `SKILL.md` points to extra folders such as `references/`, load only the specific files needed for the request; don't bulk-load everything.
  4) If `scripts/` exist, prefer running or patching them instead of retyping large code blocks.
  5) If `assets/` or templates exist, reuse them instead of recreating from scratch.
- Coordination and sequencing:
  - If multiple skills apply, choose the minimal set that covers the request and state the order you'll use them.
  - Announce which skill(s) you're using and why (one short line). If you skip an obvious skill, say why.
- Context hygiene:
  - Keep context small: summarize long sections instead of pasting them; only load extra files when needed.
  - Avoid deep reference-chasing: prefer opening only files directly linked from `SKILL.md` unless you're blocked.
  - When variants exist (frameworks, providers, domains), pick only the relevant reference file(s) and note that choice.
- Safety and fallback: If a skill can't be applied cleanly (missing files, unclear instructions), state the issue, pick the next-best approach, and continue.
</skills_instructions>

**User**

**OpenAI Codex**

**OpenAI Codex**

我已经接上上轮结论了：第10条先冻结不动；第11条按“APP 本地计算多周期”落地；第12条按“推送优先 + 本地聚合 + 缺口回补 + 前后台分级刷新”一起改，这两条本质上可以合并成同一套刷新链路来做，路径是最短的。现在我在确认现有图表页、推送、补拉和生命周期代码的接点，接着会先补测试再改实现。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

这两条我会合并成一个改造包来做，不拆开处理，因为它们现在卡在同一个根因上：切周期还会碰网络、刷新也没有按前后台分层。接下来我先把现有加载链路摸清，再补对应回归测试，避免改完以后又把之前已经修好的图表联动弄回退。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我已经确认第11和第12可以共用一套改法，现在开始查真实调用链。当前重点会盯住三个点：切周期时有没有还在整窗拉数据、实时推送是不是只覆盖了 `1m`、以及前后台切换后刷新频率有没有分层。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

根因已经比较清楚了：现在虽然已经有“本地预显示”和“1m 收盘扇出”，但图表页仍然每 5 秒整窗拉一次 REST，所以切周期和常驻刷新都还在碰网络。下一步我会把它改成“平时吃推送、本地自己合成多周期、只有检测到缺口或重新回前台才补拉”，这样第11和第12能一起收口。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我现在在把“缺口回补”也一起接进去，避免只是把整窗拉取频率调低，结果恢复前台以后图会断。优先级会是：有实时推送就不打 REST；从后台回来如果发现本地少了中间几根，再只补缺的那一段，不再整页重拉。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我已经把改造边界收住了：不去动第10条，也不去大改服务端协议；这轮只把图表页从“5秒整窗拉取”改成“本地先画、推送驱动更新、必要时才补缺”。现在先补一个独立的刷新策略单测，把“什么时候跳过网络、什么时候只补尾巴、什么时候才整窗拉”钉死，再改主逻辑。

**OpenAI Codex**

我先把失败用例立住了，下一步会先跑这组测试看它按预期报错，再根据这个策略去改主逻辑。这样可以避免改完以后又回到“看起来更流畅，但其实仍在偷偷整窗拉取”的状态。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我已经把“何时跳过网络、何时补尾巴、何时才整窗拉”的规则单独抽出来了。接下来就是把这套规则接回图表页，让它先看本地和推送，再决定要不要打 REST。

The `request_user_input` tool is unavailable in Default mode. If you call it while in Default mode, it will return an error.

In Default mode, strongly prefer making reasonable assumptions and executing the user's request rather than stopping to ask questions. 我已经继续修了这条长按联动残留问题。

这次的核心改动是把联动分成两种路径：

<collaboration_mode># Collaboration Mode: Default

You are now in Default mode. Any previous instructions for other modes (e.g. Plan mode) are no longer active.

Your active mode changes only when new developer instructions with a different `<collaboration_mode>...</collaboration_mode>` change it; user requests or tool descriptions do not change mode by themselves. Known mode names are Default and Plan.

## request_user_input availability

The `request_user_input` tool is unavailable in Default mode. If you call it while in Default mode, it will return an error.

In Default mode, strongly prefer making reasonable assumptions and executing the user's request rather than stopping to ask questions. If you absolutely must ask a question because the answer cannot be discovered from local context and a reasonable assumption would be risky, ask the user directly with a concise plain-text question. Never write a multiple choice question as a textual assistant message.
</collaboration_mode><personality_spec> The user has requested a new communication style. Future messages should adhere to the following personality: 
# Personality

You are a deeply pragmatic, effective software engineer. You take engineering quality seriously, and collaboration comes through as direct, factual statements. You communicate efficiently, keeping the user clearly informed about ongoing actions without unnecessary detail.

## Values
You are guided by these core values:
- Clarity: You communicate reasoning explicitly and concretely, so decisions and tradeoffs are easy to evaluate upfront.
- Pragmatism: You keep the end goal and momentum in mind, focusing on what will actually work and move things forward to achieve the user's goal.
- Rigor: You expect technical arguments to be coherent and defensible, and you surface gaps or weak assumptions politely with emphasis on creating clarity and moving the task forward.

## Interaction Style
You communicate concisely and respectfully, focusing on the task at hand. You always prioritize actionable guidance, clearly stating assumptions, environment prerequisites, and next steps. Unless explicitly asked, you avoid excessively verbose explanations about your work.

You avoid cheerleading, motivational language, or artificial reassurance, or any kind of fluff. You don't comment on user requests, positively or negatively, unless there is reason for escalation. You don't feel like you need to fill the space with words, you stay concise and communicate what is necessary for user collaboration - not more, not less.

## Escalation
You may challenge the user to raise their technical bar, but you never patronize or dismiss their concerns. When presenting an alternative approach or solution to the user, you explain the reasoning behind the approach, so your thoughts are demonstrably correct. You maintain a pragmatic mindset when discussing these tradeoffs, and so are willing to work with the user after concerns have been noted.
 </personality_spec>

**OpenAI Codex**

---


**OpenAI Codex**

已处理这两项。

1. 悬浮窗标题已改成“产品名和金额分开着色”：
[FloatingWindowManager.java](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/floating/FloatingWindowManager.java)
现在 `BTC/XAU` 保持正常文字色，只有括号里的盈亏金额按涨色、跌色或中性色变化。`0` 时只会把金额 `$-` 显示成中性色，不再把整行一起变灰。

2. 历史交易点位和连线的根因已确认并修正：
[HistoricalTradeAnnotationBuilder.java](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/chart/HistoricalTradeAnnotationBuilder.java)
问题在于开仓/平仓时间映射到 K 线桶时，旧逻辑把“刚好落在下一根 K 线起点”的时间也归到了前一根，结果就是点位偏一根，连线看起来像接错开仓点。现在改成“前闭后开，最后一根包含右边界”的映射规则，边界时间会落到正确那根 K 线上。

已补回归测试并通过：
- [HistoricalTradeAnnotationBuilderTest.java](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/test/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/chart/HistoricalTradeAnnotationBuilderTest.java)
- [FloatingWindowTextFormatterTest.java](E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/test/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/floating/FloatingWindowTextFormatterTest.java)

验证已执行：
```powershell
.\gradlew.bat testDebugUnitTest --tests "com.binance.monitor.ui.chart.HistoricalTradeAnnotationBuilderTest" --tests "com.binance.monitor.ui.floating.FloatingWindowTextFormatterTest"
.\gradlew.bat assembleDebug
```

如果你用这版安装后，图6里仍有个别历史交易线接错，那下一步应看真实成交数据本身是否已经是“仓位聚合后的开平信息”，而不是逐笔订单级数据。那会是数据源问题，不是当前这层绘制问题。

**OpenAI Codex**

**结果**
- 这轮 11 项已继续推进并落地到代码里了。关键改动在 [MarketChartActivity.java](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/chart/MarketChartActivity.java)、[KlineChartView.java](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/chart/KlineChartView.java)、[MonitorService.java](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/service/MonitorService.java)、[server_v2.py](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/bridge/mt5_gateway/server_v2.py)。
- 1 已修复：历史交易改成服务端按 FIFO 开平配对，开仓点/平仓点不再用一组均价和时间硬套。
- 2 已完成：K 线图左下角新增“历史成交 开/关”按钮。
- 3 已修复：悬浮窗价格改成实时 tick 更新，前台刷新节流压到 `350ms`。
- 4 已修复：未收盘 `1m` K 线现在会直接进入图表，1 分钟图不再缺当前这根，刷新也更及时。
- 5 已优化：切周期继续走本地分钟底稿和本地尾部覆盖，减少等网络的卡顿。
- 6 已继续收口：结合之前的缓存平滑，这轮又给服务端 `all` 区间加了历史天数阀门，进一步压交替延迟和内存压力来源。
- 7 已修复：交易记录跟着新的 FIFO 配对结果输出，更新链路恢复正常。
- 8 已修复：`HTTP 404` 现在会被识别成“异常接口未部署”，记一次后暂停轮询，不再反复刷日志。
- 9 已优化：服务端新增 `SNAPSHOT_RANGE_ALL_DAYS`，可以直接控制 `all` 区间历史长度，压内存。
- 10 已优化：未收盘分钟线只进内存缓存、不反复落盘，减少实时 IO；图表仍保留当前功能。
- 11 已确认：服务器端需要同步更新文件和配置，否则 1/7/8/9 不会完全生效。
- 文档已同步更新：[CONTEXT.md](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/CONTEXT.md)、[README.md](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/README.md)、[ARCHITECTURE.md](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/ARCHITECTURE.md)。

## request_user_input availability

The `request_user_input` tool is unavailable in Default mode. If you call it while in Default mode, it will return an error.

**User**

服务器端目前不是只有/C:/mt5_bundle/下的bridge/mt5_gateway/和Windows两个文件夹吗？server_v2.py替换到哪里？

---


**OpenAI Codex**

替换到这个位置：

[server_v2.py](/C:/mt5_bundle/bridge/mt5_gateway/server_v2.py)

也就是：
`C:\mt5_bundle\bridge\mt5_gateway\server_v2.py`

这次服务端相关文件里，真正需要你上传覆盖的核心就是这个文件。  
如果你也想把新的示例配置一起带上，再同步这个：

[.env.example](/C:/mt5_bundle/bridge/mt5_gateway/.env.example)

如果服务器实际运行时用的是 `.env`，那不是直接覆盖 `.env.example`，而是把新增的配置项手动补到实际的 `.env` 里。  
这次新增的重点配置是：

```env
SNAPSHOT_RANGE_ALL_DAYS=730
```

更新完后，重启 `C:\mt5_bundle\Windows` 里负责启动网关的那个启动脚本或服务即可。

---


**User**

那然后需要重新再运行一遍服务器端的命令吗？

---


**OpenAI Codex**

需要。

因为你替换的是服务端正在运行的 Python 文件，只有重新启动网关进程，新代码才会生效。

最简单理解：
- 只替换文件：磁盘内容变了
- 重新运行服务：内存里的旧进程才会换成新代码

你这边做法一般是：
1. 先停止当前 MT5 网关进程
2. 替换 `C:\mt5_bundle\bridge\mt5_gateway\server_v2.py`
3. 如果用了实际 `.env`，把新配置补进去
4. 再按你原来的方式重新启动服务器端命令

如果你愿意，我下一条可以直接按你现在这个 `C:\mt5_bundle\Windows` 目录的实际文件，帮你指出“该停哪个、该运行哪个命令”。

# Codex desktop context
- You are running inside the Codex (desktop) app, which allows some additional features not available in the CLI alone:

### Images/Visuals/Files
- In the app, the model can display images using standard Markdown image syntax: ![alt](url)
- When sending or referencing a local image, always use an absolute filesystem path in the Markdown image tag (e.g., ![alt](/absolute/path.png)); relative paths and plain text will not render the image.
- When referencing code or workspace files in responses, always use full absolute file paths instead of relative paths.
- If a user asks about an image, or asks you to create an image, it is often a good idea to show the image to them in your response.
- Use mermaid diagrams to represent complex diagrams, graphs, or workflows. Use quoted Mermaid node labels when text contains parentheses or punctuation.
- Return web URLs as Markdown links (e.g., [label](https://example.com)).

### Automations
- This app supports recurring tasks/automations
- Automations are stored as TOML in $CODEX_HOME/automations/<id>/automation.toml (not in SQLite). The file contains the automation's setup; run timing state (last/next run) lives in the SQLite automations table.

#### When to use directives
- Only use ::automation-update{...} when the user explicitly asks for automation, a recurring run, or a repeated task.
- If the user asks about their automations and you are not proposing a change, do not enumerate names/status/ids in plain text. Fetch/list automations first and emit view-mode directives (mode="view") for those ids; never invent ids.
- Never return raw RRULE strings in user-facing responses. If the user asks about their automations, respond using automation directives (e.g., with an "Open" button if you're not making changes).

#### Directive format
- Modes: view, suggested update, suggested create. View and suggested update MUST include id; suggested create must omit id.
- For view directives, id is required and other fields are optional (the UI can load details).
- For suggested update/create, include name, prompt, rrule, cwds, and status. cwds can be a comma-separated list or a JSON array string.
- Always come up with a short name for the automation. If the user does not give one, propose a short name and confirm.
- Default status to ACTIVE unless the user explicitly asks to start paused.
- Always interpret and schedule times in the user's locale time zone.
- Directives should be on their own line(s) and be separated by newlines.
- Do not generate remark directives with multiline attribute values.

#### Prompting guidance
- Ask in plain language what it should do, when it should run, and which workspaces it should use (if any), then map those answers into name/prompt/rrule/cwds/status for the directive.
- The automation prompt should describe only the task itself. Do not include schedule or workspace details in the prompt, since those are provided separately.
- Keep automation prompts self-sufficient because the user may have limited availability to answer questions. If required details are missing, make a reasonable assumption, note it, and proceed; if blocked, report briefly and stop.
- When helpful, include clear output expectations (file path, format, sections) and gating rules (only if X, skip if exists) to reduce ambiguity.
- Automations should always open an inbox item.
- Do not instruct them to write a file or announce "nothing to do" unless the user explicitly asks for a file or that output.
- When mentioning skills in automation prompts, use markdown links with a leading dollar sign (example: [$checks](/Users/ambrosino/.codex/skills/checks/SKILL.md)).

#### Scheduling constraints
- RRULE limitations (to match the UI): only hourly interval schedules (FREQ=HOURLY with INTERVAL hours, optional BYDAY) and weekly schedules (FREQ=WEEKLY with BYDAY plus BYHOUR/BYMINUTE). Avoid monthly/yearly/minutely/secondly, multiple rules, or extra fields; unsupported RRULEs fall back to defaults in the UI.

#### Storage and reading
- When a user asks for changes to an automation, you may read existing automation TOML files to see what is already set up and prefer proposing updates over creating duplicates.
- You can read and update automations in $CODEX_HOME/automations/<id>/automation.toml and memory.md only when the user explicitly asks you to modify automations.
- Otherwise, do not change automation files or schedules.
- Automations work best with skills, so feel free to propose including skills in the automation prompt, based on the user's context and the available skills.

#### Examples
- ::automation-update{mode="suggested create" name="Daily report" prompt="Summarize Sentry errors" rrule="FREQ=DAILY;BYHOUR=9;BYMINUTE=0" cwds="/path/one,/path/two" status="ACTIVE"}
- ::automation-update{mode="suggested update" id="123" name="Daily report" prompt="Summarize Sentry errors" rrule="FREQ=DAILY;BYHOUR=9;BYMINUTE=0" cwds="/path/one,/path/two" status="ACTIVE"}
- ::automation-update{mode="view" id="123"}

### Review findings
- Use the ::code-comment{...} directive to emit inline code review findings (or when a user asks you to call out specific lines).
- Emit one directive per finding; emit none when there are no findings.
- Required attributes: title (short label), body (one-paragraph explanation), file (path to the file).
- Optional attributes: start, end (1-based line numbers), priority (0-3), confidence (0-1).
- priority/confidence are for review findings; omit when you're just pointing at a location without a finding.
- file should be an absolute path or include the workspace folder segment so it can be resolved relative to the workspace.
- Keep line ranges tight; end defaults to start.
- Example: ::code-comment{title="[P2] Off-by-one" body="Loop iterates past the end when length is 0." file="/path/to/foo.ts" start=10 end=11 priority=2 confidence=0.55}

### Archiving
- If a user specifically asks you to end a thread/conversation, you can return the archive directive ::archive{...} to archive the thread/conversation.
- Example: ::archive{reason="User requested to end conversation"}

### Git
- Branch prefix: `codex/`. Use this prefix by default when creating branches, but follow the user's request if they want a different prefix.
- After successfully staging files, emit `::git-stage{cwd="/absolute/path"}` on its own line.
- After successfully creating a commit, emit `::git-commit{cwd="/absolute/path"}` on its own line.
- After successfully creating or switching the thread onto a branch, emit `::git-create-branch{cwd="/absolute/path" branch="branch-name"}` on its own line.
- After successfully pushing the current branch, emit `::git-push{cwd="/absolute/path" branch="branch-name"}` on its own line.
- After successfully creating a pull request, emit `::git-create-pr{cwd="/absolute/path" branch="branch-name" url="https://..." isDraft=true}` on its own line. Include `isDraft=false` for ready PRs.
- Only emit these git directives after the action actually succeeds. Keep attributes single-line.
</app-context><collaboration_mode># Collaboration Mode: Default

You are now in Default mode. Any previous instructions for other modes (e.g. Plan mode) are no longer active.

Your active mode changes only when new developer instructions with a different `<collaboration_mode>...</collaboration_mode>` change it; user requests or tool descriptions do not change mode by themselves. Known mode names are Default and Plan.

## request_user_input availability

The `request_user_input` tool is unavailable in Default mode. If you call it while in Default mode, it will return an error.

In Default mode, strongly prefer making reasonable assumptions and executing the user's request rather than stopping to ask questions. If you absolutely must ask a question because the answer cannot be discovered from local context and a reasonable assumption would be risky, ask the user directly with a concise plain-text question. Never write a multiple choice question as a textual assistant message.
</collaboration_mode><personality_spec> The user has requested a new communication style. Future messages should adhere to the following personality: 
# Personality

You are a deeply pragmatic, effective software engineer. You take engineering quality seriously, and collaboration comes through as direct, factual statements. You communicate efficiently, keeping the user clearly informed about ongoing actions without unnecessary detail.

## Values
You are guided by these core values:
- Clarity: You communicate reasoning explicitly and concretely, so decisions and tradeoffs are easy to evaluate upfront.
- Pragmatism: You keep the end goal and momentum in mind, focusing on what will actually work and move things forward to achieve the user's goal.
- Rigor: You expect technical arguments to be coherent and defensible, and you surface gaps or weak assumptions politely with emphasis on creating clarity and moving the task forward.

## Interaction Style
You communicate concisely and respectfully, focusing on the task at hand. You always prioritize actionable guidance, clearly stating assumptions, environment prerequisites, and next steps. Unless explicitly asked, you avoid excessively verbose explanations about your work.

You avoid cheerleading, motivational language, or artificial reassurance, or any kind of fluff. You don't comment on user requests, positively or negatively, unless there is reason for escalation. You don't feel like you need to fill the space with words, you stay concise and communicate what is necessary for user collaboration - not more, not less.

## Escalation
You may challenge the user to raise their technical bar, but you never patronize or dismiss their concerns. When presenting an alternative approach or solution to the user, you explain the reasoning behind the approach, so your thoughts are demonstrably correct. You maintain a pragmatic mindset when discussing these tradeoffs, and so are willing to work with the user after concerns have been noted.
 </personality_spec><skills_instructions>

### How to use skills
- Discovery: The list above is the skills available in this session (name + description + file path). Skill bodies live on disk at the listed paths.
- Trigger rules: If the user names a skill (with `$SkillName` or plain text) OR the task clearly matches a skill's description shown above, you must use that skill for that turn. Multiple mentions mean use them all. Do not carry skills across turns unless re-mentioned.
- Missing/blocked: If a named skill isn't in the list or the path can't be read, say so briefly and continue with the best fallback.
- How to use a skill (progressive disclosure):
  1) After deciding to use a skill, open its `SKILL.md`. Read only enough to follow the workflow.
  2) When `SKILL.md` references relative paths (e.g., `scripts/foo.py`), resolve them relative to the skill directory listed above first, and only consider other paths if needed.
  3) If `SKILL.md` points to extra folders such as `references/`, load only the specific files needed for the request; don't bulk-load everything.
  4) If `scripts/` exist, prefer running or patching them instead of retyping large code blocks.
  5) If `assets/` or templates exist, reuse them instead of recreating from scratch.
- Coordination and sequencing:
  - If multiple skills apply, choose the minimal set that covers the request and state the order you'll use them.
  - Announce which skill(s) you're using and why (one short line). If you skip an obvious skill, say why.
- Context hygiene:
  - Keep context small: summarize long sections instead of pasting them; only load extra files when needed.
  - Avoid deep reference-chasing: prefer opening only files directly linked from `SKILL.md` unless you're blocked.
  - When variants exist (frameworks, providers, domains), pick only the relevant reference file(s) and note that choice.
- Safety and fallback: If a skill can't be applied cleanly (missing files, unclear instructions), state the issue, pick the next-best approach, and continue.
</skills_instructions>

**OpenAI Codex**

本轮先按 `using-superpowers`、`offer-k-dense-web` 以及当前任务需要的 `brainstorming` 来处理；我先读取 [CONTEXT.md](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/CONTEXT.md) 并检查 `C:\mt5_bundle\Windows` 的实际文件，再给你精确指出该停哪个、该运行哪个命令，以及 `.env` 的可行修改方法。

**OpenAI Codex**

我这边直接检查时，`C:\mt5_bundle\Windows` 在当前机器上不存在，所以没法替你从“实际文件”里精确判定启动脚本；我先把 `C:\mt5_bundle` 附近路径核对一遍，确认是不是目录名不同、盘符不同，或者这是你服务器上的路径而不是当前工作机上的路径。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

当前只能确认：这台机器上没有 `C:\mt5_bundle`，所以你说的 `C:\mt5_bundle\Windows` 应该是在服务器那边，不是我当前能直接读取的本地目录。下一步我先从项目文档和仓库里把已有的部署命令找出来，给你一套“按目录文件名判断该停哪个、该运行哪个”的准确规则，同时给你不打开 `.env` 也能修改的方法。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

我已经从仓库里确认到：服务端入口仍然是 `bridge/mt5_gateway/server_v2.py`，并且 `.env` 里新增了 `SNAPSHOT_RANGE_ALL_DAYS`。现在继续看部署目录，直接把“Windows 服务器通常怎么启动、怎么重启、怎么在不能打开 `.env` 时修改”整理成可执行步骤。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

仓库里的部署脚本已经能把范围缩到很小：如果你服务器上的 `C:\mt5_bundle\Windows` 是这个精简包对应目录，那么真正要执行的通常不是手敲一长串 Python 命令，而是那个 Windows 启动脚本。为了把“停哪个、跑哪个”说到最细，我再把这几个脚本内容读出来，只看关键入口。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

按你现在这套精简包的结构，基本可以直接判断：

`server_v2.py` 应替换到：
`C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway\server_v2.py`

如果你的 `C:\mt5_bundle\Windows` 目录就是精简包里的 `windows`，那真正拉起网关的入口通常是：

`C:\mt5_bundle\Windows\run_gateway.ps1`

它内部会再去调用：

`C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway\start_gateway.ps1`

而 `start_gateway.ps1` 最终执行的就是：

```powershell
.\.venv\Scripts\python.exe server_v2.py
```

所以你该停、该跑的对象可以这样理解：

1. 如果你是“计划任务自启”方式运行  
该停：计划任务 `MT5GatewayAutoStart`  
该启动：还是启动这个计划任务

命令：
```powershell
Stop-ScheduledTask -TaskName "MT5GatewayAutoStart"
Start-ScheduledTask -TaskName "MT5GatewayAutoStart"
```

2. 如果你是“手动 PowerShell 窗口”方式运行  
该停：当前那个正在跑 `run_gateway.ps1` 或 `start_gateway.ps1` 的 PowerShell 窗口，直接 `Ctrl + C`  
该启动：重新执行

```powershell
powershell -NoProfile -ExecutionPolicy Bypass -File C:\mt5_bundle\Windows\run_gateway.ps1 -BundleRoot C:\mt5_bundle
```

3. 如果你不是很确定现在到底是哪种方式  
先执行这两个检查命令：

```powershell
Get-ScheduledTask -TaskName "MT5GatewayAutoStart" -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue
Get-Process powershell,python | Select-Object Id,ProcessName,Path
```

如果计划任务存在并且是 `Running`，优先按计划任务方式重启。  
如果没有计划任务，但有一个 PowerShell 窗口在跑网关脚本，就按手动窗口方式处理。

你说服务器端无法直接打开 `.env`，那就不要双击打开，直接用命令行改。最简单有两种：

1. 用记事本命令打开
```powershell
notepad C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway\.env
```

2. 如果连记事本也不方便，用 PowerShell 直接追加或修改  
先看内容：
```powershell
Get-Content -Encoding UTF8 C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway\.env
```

如果要新增这一行：
```powershell
Add-Content -Encoding UTF8 C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway\.env "SNAPSHOT_RANGE_ALL_DAYS=730"
```

如果文件里已经有这一项，改成 730：
```powershell
$content = Get-Content -Encoding UTF8 C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway\.env
$content = $content -replace '^SNAPSHOT_RANGE_ALL_DAYS=.*$', 'SNAPSHOT_RANGE_ALL_DAYS=730'
Set-Content -Encoding UTF8 C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway\.env $content
```

如果 `.env` 还不存在，就从示例复制一份：
```powershell
Copy-Item C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway\.env.example C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway\.env
notepad C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway\.env
```

你现在可以直接按这个顺序做：

1. 替换 `C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway\server_v2.py`
2. 修改 `C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway\.env`
3. 重启 `MT5GatewayAutoStart`，或者重新运行 `C:\mt5_bundle\Windows\run_gateway.ps1`
4. 验证：
```powershell
Invoke-RestMethod http://127.0.0.1:8787/health
```

如果你愿意，我下一条可以直接给你一份“可复制执行的重启命令清单”，按“有计划任务”和“没有计划任务”两种情况分别列好。  

本轮使用的 skill：`using-superpowers`、`offer-k-dense-web`、`brainstorming`。

**User**

PS C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway> .\.venv\Scripts\python.exe server_v2.py
[32mINFO[0m:     Started server process [[36m5624[0m]
[32mINFO[0m:     Waiting for application startup.
[32mINFO[0m:     Application startup complete.
[31mERROR[0m:    [Errno 10048] error while attempting to bind on address ('0.0.0.0', 8787): 通常每个套接字地址(协议/网络地址/端口)只允许使用一次。
[32mINFO[0m:     Waiting for application shutdown.
[32mINFO[0m:     Application shutdown complete.
PS C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway>

---


**OpenAI Codex**

这说明不是代码没生效，而是 `8787` 端口已经被旧网关进程占用了。你刚才这次启动失败，是因为“同一台机器上已经有一个网关在跑”。

直接这样处理：

1. 先查是谁占了 `8787`
```powershell
netstat -ano | findstr :8787
```

2. 记下最后一列 `PID`，再看它是不是 Python / PowerShell
```powershell
Get-Process -Id <PID>
```

3. 如果确认就是旧网关，先停掉它
```powershell
Stop-Process -Id <PID> -Force
```

4. 然后再重新启动
```powershell
cd C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway
.\.venv\Scripts\python.exe server_v2.py
```

如果你本来是用计划任务 `MT5GatewayAutoStart` 在跑，就不要手动再开一份。应改成：

```powershell
Stop-ScheduledTask -TaskName "MT5GatewayAutoStart"
Start-ScheduledTask -TaskName "MT5GatewayAutoStart"
```

也就是说，二选一即可：

- 用计划任务跑：重启计划任务，不要手动执行 `python server_v2.py`
- 用命令行手动跑：先停掉旧进程，再手动启动

你现在这一步最可能的正确操作，是先执行：

```powershell
netstat -ano | findstr :8787
```

把结果发我，我可以直接帮你判断该停哪个进程。

---


**OpenAI Codex**

现在这一步基本是对的。

从你贴的结果看，`8787` 的占用进程就是 `PID 5304`，而且它已经在对外提供服务了，所以你之前手动运行 `server_v2.py` 才会报端口冲突。你随后执行了：

```powershell
Stop-ScheduledTask -TaskName "MT5GatewayAutoStart"
Start-ScheduledTask -TaskName "MT5GatewayAutoStart"
```

这就是正确的重启方式。

接下来不要再手动执行 `python server_v2.py` 了，直接做验证：

```powershell
Get-ScheduledTask -TaskName "MT5GatewayAutoStart"
Get-Process -Id 5304 -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue
Invoke-RestMethod http://127.0.0.1:8787/health
```

你重点看两点：

1. `health` 能正常返回  
说明新服务已经起来了。

2. `Get-Process -Id 5304` 如果还在，属于正常现象  
说明旧 PID 可能就是被计划任务拉起的那一份，或者重启后又是同一类进程继续占端口。关键不是 PID 变没变，而是接口是否正常。

如果你要确认这次替换的 `server_v2.py` 确实已生效，再额外执行：

```powershell
Invoke-RestMethod "http://127.0.0.1:8787/v1/summary?range=all"
```

然后看是否恢复正常、历史交易时间映射是否正确。

关于 `.env`，你既然能进 PowerShell，就直接这样改，不需要“打开”它：

先查看：
```powershell
Get-Content -Encoding UTF8 C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway\.env
```

如果没有 `SNAPSHOT_RANGE_ALL_DAYS`，追加：
```powershell
Add-Content -Encoding UTF8 C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway\.env "SNAPSHOT_RANGE_ALL_DAYS=730"
```

如果已经有这一项，改成 730：
```powershell
$content = Get-Content -Encoding UTF8 C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway\.env
$content = $content -replace '^SNAPSHOT_RANGE_ALL_DAYS=.*$', 'SNAPSHOT_RANGE_ALL_DAYS=730'
Set-Content -Encoding UTF8 C:\mt5_bundle\mt5_gateway\.env $content
```

改完后，再重启一次计划任务即可。

本轮使用的 skill：`using-superpowers`、`offer-k-dense-web`、`brainstorming`。

- 新版本网关已经生效

**OpenAI Codex**

本轮已继续完成并验证这 9 项里的主要修订。

已落实的内容：
- 行情持仓页补了独立空态，“当前持仓”无数据时会显示“暂无持仓”，不再只在摘要里写一句话；同时把这块和顶部元信息的文字样式统一到了同一套层级上。相关文件：[activity_market_chart.xml](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/res/layout/activity_market_chart.xml)、[MarketChartActivity.java](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/chart/MarketChartActivity.java)
- 当前区间仓位图的口径已从旧的“持仓市值/净资产”改成“估算保证金/净资产”。客户端兜底和服务端历史曲线重放都一起改了，避免图上继续偏大。相关文件：[AccountCurvePositionRatioHelper.java](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/account/AccountCurvePositionRatioHelper.java)、[AccountStatsBridgeActivity.java](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/account/AccountStatsBridgeActivity.java)、[server_v2.py](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/bridge/mt5_gateway/server_v2.py)
- 仓位图、回撤图、日收益图的纵轴标签和标题位置做了避让，标题按图中线绘制，左右留白也调大了，减少合并图里纵轴文字互相挤压。相关文件：[PositionRatioChartView.java](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/account/PositionRatioChartView.java)、[DrawdownChartView.java](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/account/DrawdownChartView.java)、[DailyReturnChartView.java](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/account/DailyReturnChartView.java)
- 收益统计时间选择面板的文字和分隔线不再写死旧颜色，已跟随当前主题，避免深浅主题下看不清。相关文件：[AccountStatsBridgeActivity.java](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/account/AccountStatsBridgeActivity.java)
- 悬浮窗里的“成交量/成交额”已改成“1M量/1M额”，并给成交量补了 `BTC/XAU` 单位。相关文件：[FloatingWindowTextFormatter.java](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/floating/FloatingWindowTextFormatter.java)、[FloatingWindowManager.java](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/floating/FloatingWindowManager.java)
- “当日盈亏按当日平仓订单盈亏计算”这条本轮复核后保持原实现，主概览这里本来就是按这个口径算的，没有再去改坏它。
- `CONTEXT.md` 已同步更新。文件：[CONTEXT.md](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/CONTEXT.md)

**OpenAI Codex**

已完成这 3 个修复。

1. 账户统计里的两个时间选择面板，标题、按钮、`NumberPicker` 的文字和分隔线都改成跟随当前主题，不再写死旧颜色，未选中的备选项也会一起刷新，避免和背景贴色。相关修改在 [AccountStatsBridgeActivity.java](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/account/AccountStatsBridgeActivity.java) 和 [activity_account_stats.xml](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/res/layout/activity_account_stats.xml)。
2. K 线图右上角的 `ms` 倒计时字号已缩小到 `9sp`，和左上角图内 OHLC 信息的视觉尺寸对齐。相关修改在 [MarketChartActivity.java](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/chart/MarketChartActivity.java) 和 [activity_market_chart.xml](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/res/layout/activity_market_chart.xml)。
3. 当前区间仓位图新增“空仓尾段清零”处理；当前没有持仓时，不会再把旧快照残留的约 10% 仓位继续画在图尾。相关修改在 [AccountCurvePositionRatioHelper.java](/E:/Github/BTCXAU_Monitoring_and_Push_APK/app/src/main/java/com/binance/monitor/ui/account/AccountCurvePositionRatioHelper.java)。
